class="u-block c-link--basic u-mb--1 js-route" data-path="/reports/38275/cite" href="#" data-test-id=article_referee-report_cite-link><i class="material-icons c-link__icon">format_quote</i> <span class="u-ml--1 c-link__text">Cite this report</span></a> <a href="#report-responses-38275" class="u-block c-link--basic u-mb--1/2 js-route" data-path="/reports/38275/responses" href="#" data-test-id=article_referee-report_responses-link><i class="material-icons c-link__icon">speaker_notes</i> <span class="u-ml--1 u-mr--1/2 c-link__text u-ib">Responses</span><span class="u-black--medium u-ib u-middle">(2)</span></a> </div> <div class="u-mb--1 u-show@expanded"></div> </div> <hr class="c-hr c-hr--low u-mt--0 u-mb--2"> <div class="o-actions o-actions--middle u-mb--1"> <div class="o-actions__primary p-article__color--dark"> <span class="u-ib u-middle"> <i class="c-icn--f1r-icon c-icn--reservations" title="Approved with Reservations" #data-refInfo=272-63016></i> </span> <span class="p-article__report-status t-caption u-upper-spacing u-upper u-ib u-middle u-weight--md">Approved With Reservations</span> </div> <div class="o-actions__secondary _mdl-layout"> <div class="c-block-tip p-article__sidebar-tooltip c-block-tip--below c-block-tip--small-arrow c-block-tip--sm-padding"> <button type=button class="c-button c-button--icon c-button--text c-block-tip__toggle"><i class="material-icons c-button--icon__icon">info_outline</i></button> <div class=c-block-tip__content> <p class="t-body u-mt--0 u-mb--0"><em class=u-weight--md>Alongside their report, reviewers assign a status to the article:</em></p> <dl class=c-definitions> <dt class="c-definitions__term u-upper t-control u-weight--md u-black--high"><span class="u-ib u-middle"> <i class="c-icn--f1r-icon c-icn--approved " title=Approved #data-refInfo=""></i> </span> <span class="u-middle u-ib u-ml--1/2">Approved</span></dt> <dd class="c-definitions__description t-caption">The paper is scientifically sound in its current form and only minor, if any, improvements are suggested</dd> <dt class="c-definitions__term u-upper t-control u-weight--md u-black--high"><span class="u-ib u-middle"> <i class="c-icn--f1r-icon c-icn--reservations" title="Approved with Reservations" #data-refInfo=""></i> </span> <span class="u-middle u-ib u-ml--1/2">Approved with reservations</span></dt> <dd class="c-definitions__description t-caption"> A number of small changes, sometimes more significant revisions are required to address specific details and improve the papers academic merit. </dd> <dt class="c-definitions__term u-upper t-control u-weight--md u-black--high"><span class="u-ib u-middle"> <i class="c-icn--f1r-icon c-icn--not-approved " title="Not Approved" #data-refInfo=""></i> </span> <span class="u-middle u-ib u-ml--1/2">Not approved</span></dt> <dd class="c-definitions__description t-caption">Fundamental flaws in the paper seriously undermine the findings and conclusions</dd> </dl> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="">In the current manuscript, the authors present the first draft genome assembly for the argan tree <i>Argania spinosa</i>, a tree with significant ecological as well as commercial importance.<br/> The authors have used a hybrid assembly approach, combing data from both Illumina short-reads and PacBio long-reads technology. Use of such hybrid approaches is welcome, as they can combine the&nbsp; advantages offered by different technological platforms.<br/> Based on a k-mer analysis, the authors also provide a reasonable estimate of the genome-size and the level of heterozygosity. These are important metrics to report, as they can guide the methods to be used for genome assembly, as well as for interpretation of the assembled genome sequence. The draft genome has been satisfactorily assembled, using state of the art computational methods, and it contains 89% of the predicted core genes as defined in the BUSCO software.<br/> <br/> It is hoped that in their future studies, the authors will follow up with more improvements to the draft genome, including gene annotations using transcriptomic data.<br/> <br/> Overall, manuscript provides valuable information and sequence resources that will be useful to the scientific community.&nbsp; I have only 1 major and 6 minor comments/suggestions that I think the authors should be able to address.<br/> <br/> <b>Major reservation:</b><br/> <br/> 1. Both Illumina as well as PacBio reads have been processed and trimmed before being used as an input to the MaSuRCA software. However, the instructions for the MaSuRCA software explicitly ask for <u><b>NOT</b></u> using any third-party tools, or performing any trimming, cleaning or error correction on Illumina reads, as it will most likely lead to a deteriorated assembly&nbsp; (See https://github.com/alekseyzimin/masurca#overview). It is therefore strongly suggested that the authors try an assembly with the raw Illumina reads directly, as it might lead to a better assembly. If such an analysis was already performed but the assembly was worse than the current version, please provide this information in the manuscript.<br/> <br/> <b>Minor comment/suggestion:</b><br/> <br/> 1. For PacBio data, please specify the form of processed reads that were input to the MaSuRCA software: were they the raw PacBio reads, or the Circular Consensus Sequence&nbsp; (CCS) reads?<br/> <br/> 2. The authors report that the genomic DNA was size-selected for fragments above 2kb. What was the approximate maximum size of input DNA for PacBio library preparation. Also, what was the maximum size of PacBio reads (e.g after the CCS step) ?<br/> <br/> 3. The raw coverage obtained from Illumina data is reported as 160X. But as per my calculations, based on number of trimmed bases in table 1 and a estimated genome size of 573 Mb, I obtain 135,539,587,270 / 573,000,000 =&nbsp; 236X. Please correct or explain further.<br/> <br/> 4. In addition to the observed heterozygosity, the repeat content of the genome could be an important reason for a fragmented assembly. The k-mer analysis can also be used to estimate the % of genome that is comprised of repeats. It will be great if this estimate is provided.<br/> <br/> 5. For the BUSCO analysis, the authors report using the Arabidopsis lineage-specific orthologous groups. However, from the BUSCO manual, the only valid value for the lineage parameter seems to be âembryophyta_odb9â, which internally uses Arabidopsis hmms for Augustus-based gene predictions, but the member proteins are form multiple species. If this is the lineage parameter the authors used, please specifiy it as âembryophyta_odb9â rather than Arabidopsis, or provide more details on how the Arabidopsis BUSCO groups were determined.<br/> <br/> 6. The genome sequences of the organelles mitochondria and chloroplast are also very important in investigating the biology of any species, and also serve as important resource for evolutionary and phylogenetic studies. Therefore, it will be great if instead of completely&nbsp;removing the organellar genomes, the authors provide them as separate set of sequences, in separate files and ideally as separate GenBank entries.</div> <div class=u-mb--2> <div class=md> <div class=questionnaire> <ul class=c-questionnaire> <li class=c-questionnaire__item> <p class=c-questionnaire__question>Is the work clearly and accurately presented and does it cite the current literature?</p> <p class=c-questionnaire__answer>Yes</p> </li> <li class=c-questionnaire__item> <p class=c-questionnaire__question>Is the study design appropriate and is the work technically sound?</p> <p class=c-questionnaire__answer>Yes</p> </li> <li class=c-questionnaire__item> <p class=c-questionnaire__question>Are sufficient details of methods and analysis provided to allow replication by others?</p> <p class=c-questionnaire__answer>Yes</p> </li> <li class=c-questionnaire__item> <p class=c-questionnaire__question>If applicable, is the statistical analysis and its interpretation appropriate? </p> <p class=c-questionnaire__answer>Yes</p> </li> <li class=c-questionnaire__item> <p class=c-questionnaire__question>Are all the source data underlying the results available to ensure full reproducibility?</p> <p class=c-questionnaire__answer>Yes</p> </li> <li class=c-questionnaire__item> <p class=c-questionnaire__question>Are the conclusions drawn adequately supported by the results?</p> <p class=c-questionnaire__answer>Yes</p> </li> </ul> </div> </div> </div> <hr class="c-hr c-hr--low u-mb--2"> <h5 class="t-body u-weight--md u-mt--0 u-mb--1/2">Competing Interests</h5> <p class="u-mt--0 u-mb--2 u-italic">No competing interests were disclosed.</p> <hr class="c-hr c-hr--low u-mb--3"> <p class="u-mb--3 u-mt--0"> <strong> I confirm that I have read this submission and believe that I have an appropriate level of expertise to confirm that it is of an acceptable scientific standard, however I have significant reservations, as outlined above. </strong> </p> <div class="_mdl-layout u-mb--3"> <a href="/login?originalPath=/articles/7-1310/v2&scrollTo=referee-response-38275" class="u-1/1 mdl-button mdl-js-button mdl-button--outline mdl-button--multi-line mdl-button--colored mdl-button--white-ish" data-test-id=article_referee-report_respond><i class="material-icons u-ib u-middle">reply</i><span class="p-article__sidebar-report-respond-text u-ib u-middle">Respond to this report</span></a> </div> <hr class="c-hr c-hr--low c-hr--md u-mb--3"> <section id=report-responses-38275> <h4 class="t-h3 u-weight--md u-mb--2 u-mt--0">Responses <span class="u-weight--rg u-black--medium t-body">(2)</span></h4> <span class="c-hr c-hr--low u-mb--3"></span> <article id=referee-report-comment-4751 class="c-comment js-referee-report-comment " data-commentid=4751 data-reportid=38275 data-test-id=article_referee_report_comment> <header> <div class="c-comment__role t-caption u-black--medium" data-test-id=article_referee-report-comment_roles> <span class="u-weight--md u-upper u-ib u-mr--1/2">Author Response</span> </div> <div class="c-comment__date u-black--medium t-caption">04 May 2020</div> <h5 class="c-comment__name t-body u-weight--rg u-mt--0 u-mb--1" data-test-id=article_referee-report-comment_name> <strong class=u-weight--md>Hassan Ghazal, </strong><span class="c-comment__affiliations u-weight--rg">Faculty of Sciences, University Ibn Zohr, Agadir, Morocco, Agadir, Morocco</span> </h5> <div class="c-comment__body u-mb--1"> <div class="c-read-more js-read-more t-body" data-lines=4> <div class="c-read-more__content js-read-more-content "> <div class=u-mb--1 data-test-id=article_referee-report-comment_text data-commentid=4751>1. Both Illumina as well as PacBio reads have been processed and trimmed before being used as an input to the MaSuRCA software. However, the instructions for the MaSuRCA software explicitly ask for <b><u>NOT</u></b>&nbsp;using any third-party tools, or performing any trimming, cleaning or error correction on Illumina reads, as it will most likely lead to a deteriorated assembly&nbsp; (See https://github.com/alekseyzimin/masurca#overview). It is therefore strongly suggested that the authors try an assembly with the raw Illumina reads directly, as it might lead to a better assembly. If such an analysis was already performed but the assembly was worse than the current version, please provide this information in the manuscript.<br/> &nbsp;<br/> <b>Response</b>:<br/> Both illumina and PacBio reads have been trimmed only for adaptor removal. &nbsp;No quality trimming was performed. (The manuscript has been corrected): <ol> <li>âQuality-filtered reads from the Illuminaâ <u>has been replaced by</u> â<b>Trimmed reads from the Illumina</b>â</li> <li>âThese data was trimmed of adapters and low-quality sequences,â¦â <u>has been replaced by</u> <b>âThese data was trimmed of adapters,â¦</b>â</li> <li>âPrior to assembly, Illumina and PacBio raw reads were trimmed for quality and adaptor removal using <i>bbduk.shâ </i><u>has been&nbsp;replaced by</u><i>&nbsp;<b>â</b></i><b>Prior to assembly, Illumina raw reads and PacBio CCS reads were trimmed for adaptor removal using <i>bbduk.shâ</i></b></li> </ol> &nbsp;<br/> <b>Minor comments/suggestions:</b>&nbsp;<br/> <br/> 1. For PacBio data, please specify the form of processed reads that were input to the MaSuRCA software: were they the raw PacBio reads, or the Circular Consensus Sequence&nbsp; (CCS) reads?<b>Response:</b><br/> CCS PacBio reads were processed within MaSuRCA software<br/> <br/> 2. The authors report that the genomic DNA was size-selected for fragments above 2kb. What was the approximate maximum size of input DNA for PacBio library preparation. Also, what was the maximum size of PacBio reads (e.g after the CCS step) ?&nbsp;<br/> <br/> <b>Response:</b><br/> DNA extracted from the lyophilized leaves was divided into HMW and LMW fractions, and each was used separately to make PacBio libraries. The best PacBio SMRT cell yielded 4G of data on 163,000 spots, with an average read size of 24,468 bases.&nbsp;<br/> <br/> <br/> 3.&nbsp;The raw coverage obtained from Illumina data is reported as 160X. But as per my calculations, based on number of trimmed bases in table 1 and an estimated genome size of 573 Mb, I obtain 135,539,587,270 / 573,000,000 =&nbsp;236X. Please correct or explain further.<br/> <br/> <b>Response:</b><br/> We agree with the reviewer. The manuscript have been corrected:âThese data was trimmed of adapters and low-quality sequences, yielding a clean set of 936,053,040 reads, representing 160&times; genome coverage,â <u>has now been replaced by</u><b> âThese data was trimmed of adapters and low-quality sequences, yielding a clean set of 936,053,040 reads, representing 236x genome coverage</b>,â<br/> &nbsp;<br/> <br/> 4. In addition to the observed heterozygosity, the repeat content of the genome could be an important reason for a fragmented assembly. The k-mer analysis can also be used to estimate the % of genome that is comprised of repeats. It will be great if this estimate is provided.<br/> <br/> <b>Response:</b><br/> Based on the 21-mer distribution analysis, the duplicated fraction of the genome is estimated to be 3,19%. The revised version of the manuscript has been corrected:<br/> âThe double peak of k-mer distribution indicates heterozygosity whose rate is estimated to be 1.58 % (<a>Figure 2</a>).â <u>Has been replaced</u> by <b>âThe double peak of k-mer distribution indicates heterozygosity whose rate is estimated to be 1.58 % and the duplicated fraction of the genome is estimated to be 3,19% (<a>Figure 2</a>).â</b><br/> <br/> <br/> 5. For the BUSCO analysis, the authors report using the Arabidopsis lineage-specific orthologous groups. However, from the BUSCO manual, the only valid value for the lineage parameter seems to be âembryophyta_odb9â, which internally uses Arabidopsis hmms for Augustus-based gene predictions, but the member proteins are form multiple species. If this is the lineage parameter the authors used, please specifiy it as âembryophyta_odb9â rather than Arabidopsis, or provide more details on how the Arabidopsis BUSCO groups were determined.<br/> <br/> <b>Response:</b><br/> We agree. The lineage parameter used is âembryophyta_odb9â. (The manuscript has been corrected):<br/> âTo assess the completeness of the final assembly, a <a href="https://busco.ezlab.org/">Benchmarking Universal Single-Copy Orthologs</a>&nbsp;(BUSCO) v3 software approach was used with Arabidopsis lineage-specific orthologous groups<a>31</a>,â<u> has been replaced by</u> <b>âTo assess the completeness of the final assembly, a <a href="https://busco.ezlab.org/">Benchmarking Universal Single-Copy Orthologs</a>&nbsp;(BUSCO) v3 software approach was used with âembryophyta_odb9â lineage-specific orthologous groups<a>31</a>,</b>â<br/> &nbsp;<br/> <br/> 6.&nbsp;The genome sequences of the organelles mitochondria and chloroplast are also very important in investigating the biology of any species, and also serve as important resource for evolutionary and phylogenetic studies. Therefore, it will be great if instead of completely&nbsp;removing the organellar genomes, the authors provide them as separate set of sequences, in separate files and ideally as separate GenBank entries.&nbsp;<br/> <br/> <b>Response:</b><br/> We agree with the reviewer. The work is in progress and we plant to publish the organellar genomes soon in a separate manuscript.</div> </div> <a href="#" class="c-read-more__toggle js-read-more-toggle t-caption"> <span class=c-read-more__expand>View more</span> <span class=c-read-more__contract>View less</span> </a> </div> </div> <div class=c-comment__footer> <h5 class="t-body u-weight--md u-mt--0 u-mb--1/2">Competing Interests</h5> <p class="u-mt--0 u-mb--1 u-italic" data-test-id=article_referee-report-comment_competing-interests>The authors declare No conflict interests with this peer review.</p> </div> <footer> <div class="o-actions o-actions--middle"> <div class=o-actions__primary> <a href="/login?originalPath=/articles/7-1310/v2&scrollTo=referee-response-38275" class="c-comment js-referee-report-comment " data-commentid=5438 data-reportid=38275 data-test-id=article_referee_report_comment> <header> <div class="c-comment__role t-caption u-black--medium" data-test-id=article_referee-report-comment_roles> <span class="u-weight--md u-upper u-ib u-mr--1/2">Author Response</span> </div> <div class="c-comment__date u-black--medium t-caption">04 May 2020</div> <h5 class="c-comment__name t-body u-weight--rg u-mt--0 u-mb--1" data-test-id=article_referee-report-comment_name> <strong class=u-weight--md>Rachid Mentag, </strong><span class="c-comment__affiliations u-weight--rg">National Institute of Agricultural Research (INRA), Rabat, Morocco</span> </h5> <div class="c-comment__body u-mb--1"> <div class="c-read-more js-read-more t-body" data-lines=4> <div class="c-read-more__content js-read-more-content "> <div class=u-mb--1 data-test-id=article_referee-report-comment_text data-commentid=5438><b>Answers to Reviewer #1</b><br/> &nbsp;<br/> <b>Major reservation:</b><br/> &nbsp;<br/> 1.&nbsp;Both Illumina as well as PacBio reads have been processed and trimmed before being used as an input to the MaSuRCA software. However, the instructions for the MaSuRCA software explicitly ask for&nbsp;<b><u>NOT</u></b>&nbsp;using any third-party tools, or performing any trimming, cleaning or error correction on Illumina reads, as it will most likely lead to a deteriorated assembly&nbsp; (See https://github.com/alekseyzimin/masurca#overview). It is therefore strongly suggested that the authors try an assembly with the raw Illumina reads directly, as it might lead to a better assembly. If such an analysis was already performed but the assembly was worse than the current version, please provide this information in the manuscript.<br/> <b>Answer.</b>We agree with the reviewer. Both illumina and PacBio reads have been trimmed only for adaptor removal. No quality trimming was performed. The manuscript has been corrected:<br/> &nbsp; <ul> <li>âQuality-filtered reads from the Illuminaâ has been replaced by âTrimmed reads from the Illuminaâ</li> <li>âThese data was trimmed of adapters and low-quality sequences,â¦â has been replaced by âThese data was trimmed of adapters,â¦â</li> <li>âPrior to assembly, Illumina and PacBio raw reads were trimmed for quality and adaptor removal using bbduk.shâ has beenreplaced by âPrior to assembly, Illumina raw reads and PacBio CCS reads were trimmed for adaptor removal using bbduk.shâ&nbsp;</li> </ul> <b>Minor comment/suggestion:</b><br/> <br/> 1-&nbsp;For PacBio data, please specify the form of processed reads that were input to the MaSuRCA software: were they the raw PacBio reads, or the Circular Consensus Sequence&nbsp; (CCS) reads?&nbsp;<br/> <b>Answer</b>. CCS PacBio reads were processed within MaSuRCA software. The manuscript has been corrected:<br/> &nbsp; <ul> <li>âPrior to assembly,&nbsp;Short and long reads wereâ¦â has been replaced by âPrior to assembly, Illumina raw reads and PacBio CCS reads were&nbsp;â¦â</li> </ul> <br/> 2-&nbsp;The authors report that the genomic DNA was size-selected for fragments above 2kb. What was the approximate maximum size of input DNA for PacBio library preparation. Also, what was the maximum size of PacBio reads (e.g after the CCS step) ?&nbsp;<br/> <b>Answer</b>.DNA extracted from the lyophilized leaves was divided into HMW and LMW fractions, and each was used separately to make PacBio libraries. The best PacBio SMRT cell yielded 4G of data on 163,000 spots, with an average read size of 24,468 bases.<br/> &nbsp;<br/> 3- The raw coverage obtained from Illumina data is reported as 160X. But as per my calculations, based on number of trimmed bases in table 1 and a estimated genome size of 573 Mb, I obtain 135,539,587,270 / 573,000,000 =&nbsp;236X. Please correct or explain further.&nbsp;<br/> <b>Answer</b>.We agree with the reviewer. The manuscript have been corrected:<br/> &nbsp; <ul> <li>ââ¦.yielding a clean set of 936,053,040 reads, representing 160&times; genome coverage,â has now been replaced by ââ¦yielding a clean set of 936,053,040 reads, representing 236x genome coverage,â</li> </ul> &nbsp;<br/> 4- In addition to the observed heterozygosity, the repeat content of the genome could be an important reason for a fragmented assembly. The k-mer analysis can also be used to estimate the % of genome that is comprised of repeats. It will be great if this estimate is provided.&nbsp;<br/> <b>Answer</b>.Based on the 21-mer distribution analysis, the duplicated fraction of the genome is estimated to be 3,19%. The revised version of the manuscript has been corrected:<br/> &nbsp; <ul> <li>âThe double peak of k-mer distribution indicates heterozygosity whose rate is estimated to be 1.58 % (<a href="https://f1000research.com/articles/7-1310/v1#f2">Figure 2</a>).â Has been replaced by âThe double peak of k-mer distribution indicates heterozygosity whose rate is estimated to be 1.58 % and the duplicated fraction of the genome is estimated to be 3,19% (<a href="https://f1000research.com/articles/7-1310/v1#f2">Figure 2</a>).â</li> </ul> &nbsp;<br/> 5- For the BUSCO analysis, the authors report using the Arabidopsis lineage-specific orthologous groups. However, from the BUSCO manual, the only valid value for the lineage parameter seems to be âembryophyta_odb9â, which internally uses Arabidopsis hmms for Augustus-based gene predictions, but the member proteins are form multiple species. If this is the lineage parameter the authors used, please specifiy it as âembryophyta_odb9â rather than Arabidopsis, or provide more details on how the Arabidopsis BUSCO groups were determined.&nbsp;<br/> <b>Answer</b>. We agree with the reviewer. The lineage parameter used was âembryophyta_odb9â. The manuscript has been corrected:<br/> &nbsp; <ul> <li>âTo assess the completeness of the final assembly, a&nbsp;<a href="https://busco.ezlab.org/">Benchmarking Universal Single-Copy Orthologs</a>&nbsp;(BUSCO) v3 software approach was used with Arabidopsis lineage-specific orthologous groups...â has been replaced by âTo assess the completeness of the final assembly, a&nbsp;<a href="https://busco.ezlab.org/">Benchmarking Universal Single-Copy Orthologs</a>&nbsp;(BUSCO) v3 software approach was used with âembryophyta_odb9â lineage-specific orthologous groups...â</li> </ul> &nbsp;<br/> 6- The genome sequences of the organelles mitochondria and chloroplast are also very important in investigating the biology of any species, and also serve as important resource for evolutionary and phylogenetic studies. Therefore, it will be great if instead of completely&nbsp;removing the organellar genomes, the authors provide them as separate set of sequences, in separate files and ideally as separate GenBank entries.&nbsp;<br/> <b>Answer</b>.We agree with the reviewer. The work is in progress and we plan to publish the organellar genomes soon in separate manuscripts.</div> </div> <a href="#" class="c-read-more__toggle js-read-more-toggle t-caption"> <span class=c-read-more__expand>View more</span> <span class=c-read-more__contract>View less</span> </a> </div> </div> <div class=c-comment__footer> <h5 class="t-body u-weight--md u-mt--0 u-mb--1/2">Competing Interests</h5> <p class="u-mt--0 u-mb--1 u-italic" data-test-id=article_referee-report-comment_competing-interests>No competing interests were disclosed.</p> </div> <footer> <div class="o-actions o-actions--middle"> <div class=o-actions__primary> <a href="/login?originalPath=/articles/7-1310/v2&scrollTo=referee-response-38275" class="js-referee-report-comment c-link--basic" data-test-id=article_referee-report-comment_respond><i class="material-icons c-link__icon">reply</i> <span class=c-link__text>Respond</span></a> </div> <div class=o-actions__secondary> <a href="mailto:research@f1000.com?subject=Report a concern (15719) " data-test-id=article_referee-report-comment_concern class="js-report-concern t-caption c-link c-link--inline">Report a concern</a> </div> </div> </footer> </header> </article> </section> <script type="text/template" data-template=refereeReportCitation-38275 id=refereeReportCitation-38275 class=u-hide>

your comments might lead a reasonable person to question your impartiality. personal relationship (e.g. parent, spouse, sibling, or domestic partner) with any of the authors.</li> <li class=standard-padding>You are a close professional associate of any of the authors (e.g. scientific mentor, recent student).</li> <li class=standard-padding>You work at the same institute as any of the authors.</li> <li class=standard-padding>You hope/expect to benefit (e.g. favour or employment) as a result of your submission.</li> <li class=standard-padding>You are an Editor for the journal in which the article is published.</li> </ol> <div class="heading5 padding-top">Examples of 'Financial Competing Interests'</div> <ol class="numbered-list no-padding"> <li class=standard-padding>You expect to receive, or in the past 4 years have received, any of the following from any received, shared grant support or other funding with any of the authors.</li> <li class=standard-padding>You hold, or are currently applying for, any patents or significant stocks/shares relating to id=article-competing-intersts-policy class=js-article-competing-interests-policy style="display: none;"> <h2 class="h2-title u-mt--0 u-pt--0">Competing Interests Policy</h2> <p> Provide sufficient details of any financial or non-financial competing interests to enable users to assess whether your comments might lead a reasonable person to question your impartiality. Consider the following examples, but note that this is not an exhaustive list: </p> <div class=heading5>Examples of 'Non-Financial Competing Interests'</div> <ol class="numbered-list no-padding"> <li class=standard-padding>Within the past 4 years, you have held joint grants, published or collaborated with any of the authors of the selected paper.</li> <li class=standard-padding>You have a close personal relationship (e.g. parent, spouse, sibling, or domestic partner) with any of the authors.</li> <li class=standard-padding>You are a close professional associate of any of the authors (e.g. scientific mentor, recent student).</li> <li class=standard-padding>You work at the same institute as any of the authors.</li> <li class=standard-padding>You hope/expect to benefit (e.g. favour or employment) as a result of your submission.</li> <li class=standard-padding>You are an Editor for the journal in which the article is published.</li> </ol> <div class="heading5 padding-top">Examples of 'Financial Competing Interests'</div> <ol class="numbered-list no-padding"> <li class=standard-padding>You expect to receive, or in the past 4 years have received, any of the following from any commercial organisation that may gain financially from your submission: a salary, fees, funding, reimbursements.</li> <li class=standard-padding>You expect to receive, or in the past 4 years have received, shared grant support or other funding with any of the authors.</li> <li class=standard-padding>You hold, or are currently applying for, any patents or significant stocks/shares relating to 	$(function(){
		// Note: All the setup needs to run against a name attribute and *not* the id due the clonish
		// nature of facebox...
		$("a[id=googleSignInButton]").click(function(event){
            event.preventDefault();
            $("input[id=oAuthSystem]").val("GOOGLE");
            $("form[id=oAuthForm]").submit();
        });
        $("a[id=facebookSignInButton]").click(function(event){
            event.preventDefault();
            $("input[id=oAuthSystem]").val("FACEBOOK");
            $("form[id=oAuthForm]").submit();
        });
        $("a[id=orcidSignInButton]").click(function(event){
            event.preventDefault();
            $("input[id=oAuthSystem]").val("ORCID");
            $("form[id=oAuthForm]").submit();
        });
	});
</script>

        if (uris.pop() === "login") {

        }
    });
});
